How does the Einstein Trust Layer ensure that sensitive data is protected while generating useful and meaningful responses?


Einstein ä¿¡ä»»å±¤å¦‚ä½•ç¢ºä¿åœ¨ç”Ÿæˆæœ‰ç”¨ä¸”æœ‰æ„ç¾©çš„å›è¦†æ™‚ä¿è­·æ•æ„Ÿè³‡æ–™ï¼Ÿ


A. Masked data will be de-masked during response journey.

è¢«é®ç½©çš„è³‡æ–™å°‡åœ¨å›è¦†éç¨‹ä¸­è¢«è§£é™¤é®ç½© (de-masked)ã€‚

What is automatically created when a custom search index is created in Data Cloud?

What is the primary function of the planner service in the Agent system?

A. Generating record queries based on conversation history

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The primary function of the planner service in the Agent system is to identify copilot actions that should be taken in response to user utterances. This service is responsible for analyzing the conversation and determining the appropriate actions (such as querying records, generating a response, or taking another action).

Universal Containers (UC) plans to answer questions based on similar cases that have been successfully resolved in the past.
What should UC consider when implementing this approach?

C. Create an unstructured data model object (UDMO) based on Case object and create an index on it.

åŸºæ–¼ Case ç‰©ä»¶å»ºç«‹éçµæ§‹åŒ–è³‡æ–™æ¨¡å‹ç‰©ä»¶ (UDMO) ä¸¦ç‚ºå…¶å»ºç«‹ç´¢å¼•ã€‚

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):

Universal Containers is indexing millions of product manuals where users may ask both structured queries (model numbers) and natural language questions (for example, "How do I reset my device?"), Which retrieval approach should the company use?


Universal Containers æ­£åœ¨ç´¢å¼•æ•¸ç™¾è¬ä»½ç”¢å“æ‰‹å†Šï¼Œä½¿ç”¨è€…å¯èƒ½æœƒè©¢å•çµæ§‹åŒ–æŸ¥è©¢ï¼ˆå‹è™Ÿï¼‰å’Œè‡ªç„¶èªè¨€å•é¡Œï¼ˆä¾‹å¦‚ï¼Œã€Œå¦‚ä½•é‡ç½®æˆ‘çš„è£ç½®ï¼Ÿã€ï¼‰ã€‚å…¬å¸æ‡‰ä½¿ç”¨å“ªç¨®æª¢ç´¢æ–¹æ³•ï¼Ÿ


A. Use keyword search only, since model numbers dominate queries.

åƒ…ä½¿ç”¨é—œéµå­—æœå°‹ï¼Œå› ç‚ºå‹è™Ÿä¸»å°æŸ¥è©¢ã€‚

B. Use semantic search only, as natural language is always preferred.

åƒ…ä½¿ç”¨èªæ„æœå°‹ï¼Œå› ç‚ºè‡ªç„¶èªè¨€ç¸½æ˜¯é¦–é¸ã€‚

C. Use hybrid search to combine keyword precision with semantic flexibility.

ä½¿ç”¨æ··åˆæœå°‹ (hybrid search) ä¾†çµåˆé—œéµå­—ç²¾ç¢ºåº¦èˆ‡èªæ„éˆæ´»æ€§ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Hybrid search combines the precision of keyword retrieval for structured terms, such as IDs or model numbers, with the semantic flexibility of vector search for natural language queries. This approach ensures both deterministic accuracy and contextual understanding.

é¢å°æ··åˆé¡å‹çš„æŸ¥è©¢éœ€æ±‚ï¼ˆç²¾ç¢ºçš„å‹è™Ÿ vs. æ¨¡ç³Šçš„è‡ªç„¶èªè¨€å•é¡Œï¼‰ï¼Œã€Œæ··åˆæœå°‹ (Hybrid Search)ã€æ˜¯æœ€ä½³è§£æ±ºæ–¹æ¡ˆã€‚å®ƒåŒæ™‚åˆ©ç”¨é—œéµå­—ç´¢å¼•ä¾†ç²¾ç¢ºåŒ¹é…å‹è™Ÿï¼Œä»¥åŠå‘é‡ç´¢å¼•ä¾†ç†è§£è‡ªç„¶èªè¨€å•é¡Œçš„èªæ„ï¼Œå¾è€Œæä¾›æœ€å…¨é¢ä¸”æº–ç¢ºçš„æª¢ç´¢çµæœã€‚

Which statement explains why a company might prefer a hybrid search index in Data Cloud for Agentforce?

A. Hybrid search indexes process queries faster than vector search because they eliminate the need for semantic embedding.

æ··åˆæœå°‹ç´¢å¼•è™•ç†æŸ¥è©¢çš„é€Ÿåº¦æ¯”å‘é‡æœå°‹å¿«ï¼Œå› ç‚ºå®ƒå€‘æ¶ˆé™¤äº†å°èªæ„åµŒå…¥çš„éœ€æ±‚ã€‚

æ··åˆæœå°‹ä¸­çš„å‘é‡åµŒå…¥é€éé—œéµå­—åŒ¹é…é€²è¡Œé ç¯©é¸ï¼Œæ¸›å°‘äº†è¨ˆç®—é–‹éŠ·ä¸¦æé«˜äº†å›æ‡‰æº–ç¢ºæ€§ã€‚

æ··åˆæœå°‹ç´¢å¼•æ”¯æ´å­—é¢é—œéµå­—åŒ¹é…å’Œèªæ„å¬å›ï¼Œç•¶æŸ¥è©¢æ··åˆäº†ç‰¹å®šè¡“èªå’Œæ„åœ–æ™‚éå¸¸æœ‰ç”¨ã€‚

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Hybrid search indexes are preferred when organizations need both literal keyword matching and semantic understanding for complex, natural-language queries. It combines the precision of keywords with the contextual understanding of vector search.
